问题ID: 4
问题内容: What is the closest palindrome number to the year the brother of this first round draft pick by the Washington Redskins was drafted?
预期答案: 2002
系统答案: 目前无法确定华盛顿红皮队某位第一轮选秀球员的兄弟被选中的年份，因为现有工具均要求预先提供具体的运动员姓名，而无法通过“团队 + 轮次”条件枚举符合条件的第一轮选秀球员。此外，家庭关系查询工具也需要明确的球员名称作为输入，导致无法自动遍历或发现相关兄弟关系。因此，整个查询链条在初始阶段受阻，无法推进至获取选秀年份并计算最近回文数的步骤。

最终答案：**无法确定，因工具限制导致关键信息不可达。**
结果: ❌ 错误

问题ID: 820
问题内容: The submission deadline is at 17 November 1983, 04:00, Anywhere on Earth (AoE). At what date and time is the deadline in the place of birth of the director of film Boden'S Boy?
预期答案: 1983-11-17 16:00
系统答案: The deadline of 17 November 1983, 04:00 AoE corresponds to **16:00 GMT** on the same day in Weston-super-Mare, Somerset, the birthplace of Henry Edwards, director of *Boden's Boy*. This is because AoE (UTC-12) is 12 hours behind UTC, making the time 16:00 UTC, and since the UK was on GMT (UTC+0) at that date (after daylight saving ended on 2 October), the local time in Weston-super-Mare was 16:00.
结果: ✅ 正确
